<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">3 Duets for Clarinet and Bassoon
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Beethoven,_Ludwig_van" title="Category:Beethoven, Ludwig van">Beethoven, Ludwig van</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>WoO 27
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>ILB 50
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td><i>see below</i>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 duets:
<ol><li> Duet (C&#160;major)
<dl><dd>Allegro commodo (C&#160;major)
</dd><dd>Larghetto sostenuto (C&#160;minor)
</dd><dd>Rondo. Allegretto (C&#160;major)
</dd></dl>
</li><li> Duet (F&#160;major)
<dl><dd>Allegro affettuoso (F&#160;major)
</dd><dd>Aria. Larghetto (D&#160;minor)
</dd><dd>Rondo. Allegro moderato (F&#160;major)
</dd></dl>
</li><li> Duet (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
<dl><dd>Allegro sostenuto (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</dd><dd>Aria con variazioni. Andantino con moto (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</dd></dl>
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1790-92
